TOO_FEW (rb_raise(rb_eArgError, toofew), 0)\n#define THISFROM (items > 0 ? RARRAY_PTR(ary)[idx] : TOO_FEW)\n#define NEXTFROM (items-- > 0 ? RARRAY_PTR(ary)[idx++] : TOO_FEW)\n\n    while (p < pend) {\n        int explicit_endian = 0;\n        if (RSTRING_PTR(fmt) + RSTRING_LEN(fmt) != pend) {\n            rb_raise(rb_eRuntimeError, \"format string modified\");\n        }\n        type = *p++;           /* get data type */\n#ifdef NATINT_PACK\n        natint = 0;\n#endif\n\n        if (ISSPACE(type)) continue;\n        if (type == '#') {\n            while ((p < pend) && (*p != '\\n')) {\n                p++;\n            }\n            continue;\n        }\n\n        {\n            static const char natstr[] = \"sSiIlL\";\n            static const char endstr[] = \"sSiIlLqQ\";\n\n          modifiers:\n            switch (*p) {\n              case '_':\n              case '!':\n                if (strchr(natstr, type)) {\n#ifdef NATINT_PACK\n                    natint = 1;\n#endif\n                    p++;\n                }\n                else {\n                    rb_raise(rb_eArgError, \"'%c' allowed only after types %s\", *p, natstr);\n                }\n                goto modifiers;\n\n              case '<':\n              case '>':\n                if (!strchr(endstr, type)) {\n and '>'\");\n                }\n                explicit_endian = *p++;\n                goto modifiers;\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (*p == '*') {       /* set data length */\n            len = strchr(\"@Xxu\", type) ? 0\n                : strchr(\"PMm\", type) ? 1\n                : items;\n            p++;\n        }\n        else if (ISDIGIT(*p)) {\n            errno = 0;\n            len = STRTOUL(p, (char**)&p, 10);\n            if (errno) {\n                rb_raise(rb_eRangeError, \"pack length too big\");\n            }\n        }\n        else {\n            len = 1;\n        }\n\n        switch (type) {\n          case 'U':\n            /* if encoding is US-ASCII, upgrade to UTF-8 */\n            if (enc_info == 1) enc_info = 2;\n            break;\n          case 'm': case 'M': case 'u':\n            /* keep US-ASCII (do nothing) */\n            break;\n          default:\n            /* fall back to BINARY */\n            enc_info = 0;\n            break;\n        }\n        switch (type) {\n          case 'A': case 'a': case 'Z':\n          case 'B': case 'b':\n          case 'H': case 'h':\n            from = NEXTFROM;\n            if (NIL_P(from)) {\n                ptr = \"\";\n                plen = 0;\n            }\n            else {\n                StringValue(from);\n                ptr = RSTRING_PTR(from);\n                plen = RSTRING_LEN(from);\n                OBJ_INFECT(res, from);\n            }\n\n            if (p[-1] == '*')\n                len = plen;\n\n            switch (type) {\n              case 'a':                /* arbitrary binary string (null padded)  */\n              case 'A':         /* arbitrary binary string (ASCII space padded) */\n              case 'Z':         /* null terminated string  */\n                if (plen >= len) {\n                    rb_str_buf_cat(res, ptr, len);\n                    if (p[-1] == '*' && type == 'Z')\n                        rb_str_buf_cat(res, nul10, 1);\n                }\n                else {\n                    rb_str_buf_cat(res, ptr, plen);\n                    len -= plen;\n                    while (len >= 10) {\n                        rb_str_buf_cat(res, (type == 'A')?spc10:nul10, 10);\n                        len -= 10;\n                    }\n                    rb_str_buf_cat(res, (type == 'A')?spc10:nul10, len);\n                }\n                break;\n\n#define castchar(from) (char)((from) & 0xff)\n\n              case 'b':                /* bit string (ascending) */\n                {\n                    int byte = 0;\n                    long i, j = 0;\n\n                    if (len > plen) {\n                        j = (len - plen + 1)/2;\n                        len = plen;\n                    }\n                    for (i=0; i++ < len; ptr++) {\n                        if (*ptr & 1)\n                            byte |= 128;\n                        if (i & 7)\n                            byte >>= 1;\n                        else {\n                            char c = castchar(byte);\n                            rb_str_buf_cat(res, &c, 1);\n                            byte = 0;\n                        }\n                    }\n                    if (len & 7) {\n                        char c;\n                        byte >>= 7 - (len & 7);\n                        c = castchar(byte);\n                        rb_str_buf_cat(res, &c, 1);\n                    }\n                    len = j;\n                    goto grow;\n                }\n                break;\n\n              case 'B':                /* bit string (descending) */\n                {\n                    int byte = 0;\n                    long i, j = 0;\n\n                    if (len > plen) {\n                        j = (len - plen + 1)/2;\n                        len = plen;\n                    }\n                    for (i=0; i++ < len; ptr++) {\n                        byte |= *ptr & 1;\n                rb_raise(rb_eRangeError, \"too big to product\");\n            resultlen *= k;\n        }\n        result = rb_ary_new2(resultlen);\n    }\n    for (;;) {\n        int m;\n        /* sym_random, randgen);\n    }\n    ptr = RARRAY_PTR(ary);\n    len = RARRAY_LEN(ary);\n    if (argc == 0) {\n        if (len == 0) return Qnil;\n        if (len == 1) {\n            i = 0;\n        }\n        else {\n            i = RAND_UPTO(len);\n            if ((len = RARRAY_LEN(ary)) <= i) return Qnil;\n            ptr = RARRAY_PTR(ary);\n        }\n        return ptr[i];\n    }\n    rb_scan_args(argc, argv, \"1\", &nv);\n    n = NUM2LONG(nv);\n    if (n < 0) rb_raise(rb_eArgError, \"negative sample number\");\n    if (n > len) n = len;\n    if (n <= numberof(idx)) {\n        for (i = 0; i < n; ++i) {\n            rnds[i] = RAND_UPTO(len - i);\n        }\n    }\n    k = len;\n    len = RARRAY_LEN(ary);\n    ptr = RARRAY_PTR(ary);\n    if (len < k) {\n        if (n <= numberof(idx)) {\n            for (i = 0; i < n; ++i) {\n                if (rnds[i] >= len) {\n                    return rb_ary_new2(0);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    if (n > len) n = len;\n    switch (n) {\n      case 0:\n        return rb_ary_new2(0);\n      case 1:\n        i = rnds[0];\n        return rb_ary_new4(1, &ptr[i]);\n      case 2:\n        i = rnds[0];\n        j = rnds[1];\n        if (j >= i) j++;\n        return rb_ary_new3(2, ptr[i], ptr[j]);\n      case 3:\n        i = rnds[0];\n        j = rnds[1];\n        k = rnds[2];\n        {\n
